  current progress
  The Dockerfile has been created with most required tools and dependencies installed. All necessary directories have been created, and most configuration files have been generated. However, the build failed due to a syntax error in the .bazelrc file creation section where the heredoc syntax was incorrectly parsed by Docker.
  next step
  Fix the .bazelrc file creation by escaping the EOF delimiter or using a different approach. Replace the problematic section (lines 112-115) with:
  ```dockerfile
  RUN echo 'build --cxxopt=-std=c++11' > .bazelrc && \
      echo 'build --host_cxxopt=-std=c++11' >> .bazelrc
  ```

NEXT:
  current progress
  The Dockerfile has been created with most of the required software installations and file creations. However, the build failed due to a syntax error in the .clang-format file creation. The RUN command for creating .clang-format is incorrectly formatted - the heredoc content is being interpreted as Dockerfile instructions rather than file content.
  next step
  Fix the .clang-format file creation by properly formatting the RUN command with correct heredoc syntax. Change lines 115-118 from:
  ```
  RUN cat > .clang-format << 'EOF'
  BasedOnStyle: LLVM
  IndentWidth: 4
  EOF
  ```
  To:
  ```
  RUN cat > .clang-format << 'EOF' \
  BasedOnStyle: LLVM \
  IndentWidth: 4 \
  EOF
  ```
  Or use a single-line echo command:
  ```
  RUN echo -e "BasedOnStyle: LLVM\nIndentWidth: 4" > .clang-format
  ```

      ],
      targets: [

      ]
  )
  EOF
  RUN cat > test_spm/Sources/test_spm/main.swift << 'EOF'
  import Foundation
  print("Swift Package Manager test")
  EOF
  RUN cat > test_spm_objc/Package.swift << 'EOF'
  // swift-tools-version:5.9
  import PackageDescription
  let package = Package(
      name: "test_spm_objc",
      dependencies: [
          .package(url: "https://github.com/nlohmann/json.git", from: "3.11.3")
      ],
      targets: [
          .target(
              name: "test_spm_objc",
              dependencies: [.product(name: "nlohmann-json", package: "json")]
          )
      ]
  )
  EOF
  RUN cat > test_spm_objc/Sources/test_spm_objc/test.mm << 'EOF'

      nlohmann::json j = {{"test", "value"}};
  }
  EOF
  RUN cat > test_fetchcontent/CMakeLists.txt << 'EOF'
  cmake_minimum_required(VERSION 3.14)
  project(test_fetchcontent)
  include(FetchContent)

      json
      GIT_REPOSITORY https://github.com/nlohmann/json.git
      GIT_TAG v3.11.3
  )

  EOF
  RUN cat > test_modules/CMakeLists.txt << 'EOF'
  cmake_minimum_required(VERSION 3.28)

  set(CMAKE_CXX_STANDARD_REQUIRED ON)
  find_package(nlohmann_json REQUIRED)
  add_executable(test_modules test.cpp)
  target_link_libraries(test_modules nlohmann_json::nlohmann_json)
  EOF
  RUN cat > test_arm/test_arm_build.sh << 'EOF'
  #!/bin/bash
  docker build -f docker/Dockerfile.arm -t json-arm-test .
  docker run --rm json-arm-test
  EOF
  RUN chmod +x test_arm/test_arm_build.sh
  RUN cat > docker/Dockerfile.arm << 'EOF'

  EOF

  current progress
  The Dockerfile has been created with most of the required software installations and file creations. However, the build failed due to a syntax error in the .astylerc file creation. The error occurred because the heredoc syntax was not properly formatted - the content lines were interpreted as Dockerfile instructions instead of being part of the file content.
  next step
  Fix the .astylerc file creation by using proper heredoc syntax or echo commands. Replace the current .astylerc creation block (lines 117-120) with:
  ```
  RUN echo '--style=allman' > .astylerc && \
      echo '--indent=spaces=4' >> .astylerc
  ```
  This will properly create the .astylerc configuration file with the required formatting options for the astyle code formatter.

DOCKERFILE:
  FROM ubuntu:22.04
  ENV DEBIAN_FRONTEND=noninteractive
  ENV TZ=UTC
  RUN apt-get update && apt-get install -y --no-install-recommends \
      build-essential \
      git \
      wget \
      curl \
      unzip \
      make \
      pkg-config \
      libssl-dev \
      locales \
      gcc-multilib \
      g++-multilib \
      python3 \
      python3-pip \
      python3-venv \
      ninja-build \
      lcov \
      valgrind \
      doxygen \
      clang \
      clang-tools \
      libc++ \
      libc++-dev \
      software-properties-common \
      apt-transport-https \
      ca-certificates \
      gnupg \
      lsb-release \
      && rm -rf /var/lib/apt/lists/*
  RUN locale-gen en_US.UTF-8
  ENV LANG=en_US.UTF-8
  ENV LANGUAGE=en_US:en
  ENV LC_ALL=en_US.UTF-8
  RUN wget -O - https://apt.kitware.com/keys/kitware-archive-latest.asc 2>/dev/null | gpg --dearmor - | tee /etc/apt/trusted.gpg.d/kitware.gpg >/dev/null && \
      apt-add-repository "deb https://apt.kitware.com/ubuntu/ $(lsb_release -cs) main" && \
      apt-get update && \
      apt-get install -y cmake && \
      rm -rf /var/lib/apt/lists/*
  RUN pip3 install --upgrade pip setuptools wheel
  RUN pip3 install \
      meson==1.3.0 \
      PyYAML==6.0.2 \
      watchdog==6.0.0 \
      jinja2==3.1.6 \
      MkDocs==1.6.1 \
      mkdocs-git-revision-date-localized-plugin==1.4.7 \
      mkdocs-material==9.6.18 \
      mkdocs-material-extensions==1.3.1 \
      mkdocs-minify-plugin==0.8.0 \
      mkdocs-redirects==1.2.2 \
      mkdocs-htmlproofer-plugin==1.3.0 \
      cppcheck==1.5.0 \
      cpplint==2.0.2 \
      reuse==5.0.2 \
      astyle==3.4.13 \
      coveralls
  RUN wget https://github.com/bazelbuild/bazelisk/releases/latest/download/bazelisk-linux-amd64 -O /usr/local/bin/bazel && \
      chmod +x /usr/local/bin/bazel
  RUN git clone https://github.com/emscripten-core/emsdk.git /opt/emsdk && \
      cd /opt/emsdk && \
      ./emsdk install latest && \
      ./emsdk activate latest
  ENV PATH="/opt/emsdk:/opt/emsdk/upstream/emscripten:${PATH}"
  RUN wget https://swift.org/builds/swift-5.9.2-release/ubuntu2204/swift-5.9.2-RELEASE/swift-5.9.2-RELEASE-ubuntu22.04.tar.gz && \
      tar xzf swift-5.9.2-RELEASE-ubuntu22.04.tar.gz && \
      mv swift-5.9.2-RELEASE-ubuntu22.04 /opt/swift && \
      rm swift-5.9.2-RELEASE-ubuntu22.04.tar.gz
  ENV PATH="/opt/swift/usr/bin:${PATH}"
  RUN git clone https://github.com/google/benchmark.git /opt/benchmark && \
      cd /opt/benchmark && \
      cmake -E make_directory "build" && \
      cmake -E chdir "build" cmake -DBENCHMARK_DOWNLOAD_DEPENDENCIES=on -DCMAKE_BUILD_TYPE=Release .. && \
      cmake --build "build" --config Release && \
      cmake --install "build" --config Release
  WORKDIR /workspace
  COPY . /workspace/
  RUN cd /workspace && \
      mkdir -p build && \
      cd build && \
      cmake .. -DJSON_BuildTests=ON && \
      make -j$(nproc)
  CMD ["/bin/bash"]

  ENV LANGUAGE=en_US:en
  ENV LC_ALL=en_US.UTF-8

      apt-add-repository "deb https://apt.kitware.com/ubuntu/ $(lsb_release -cs) main" && \
      apt-get update && \
      apt-get install -y cmake && \
      rm -rf /var/lib/apt/lists/*
  RUN pip3 install --upgrade pip setuptools wheel
  RUN pip3 install \

      chmod +x /usr/local/bin/bazel
